          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            HakkÄ±mÄ±zda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              As Yongatek Microelectronics, we develop our own IPs and SoCs/chips in the fields of AI, 5G and IoT. We provide products and services as a 'FPGA/ASIC Design and Verification House' for major global players. Our offerings span across a diverse spectrum, encompassing IC/ASIC/SoC/FPGA/Chip Design, 5G/6G and Satellite Communications, AI-Based Video Processing, IoT and Automation, Quality Control Systems for Industry 4.0, and Defence sectors. This wide array of services is powered by our accomplished and skilled R&amp;D team. We are currently focusing on five core areas.  
 

DIGITAL DESIGN AND ADVANCED VERIFICATION  

- ASIC &amp; FPGA Design and Verification  
- RISC-V and Arm based SoC design , ASIC front-end implementation  
- Experience in following protocols/standards: AMBA,TileLink, MIPI, Ethernet,USB, CAN, UART, I2C, SPI, PWM  
- DO-254 Avionics Compliance, Advanced UVM Verification  
- Advanced Functional Verification 
- Design Validation  
- Requirement Management 
- Training (Digital Design, FPGA Design, UVM Verification) 

ELECTRONIC SYSTEM DESIGN AND VERIFICATION  

- System Architecture and PCB Design, Firmware/Software Design 
- System Integration, Test and Verification  
 
COMMUNICATION  

- 5G New Radio 
- O-RAN  
- LDPC  
- MIMO  
- Satellite Communication (SATCOM) 
- WLAN 
- Bluetooth 

 
COMPUTER VISION AND REAL TIME IMAGE PROCESSING  

- Python / C++ / OpenCV / Pytorch / Cuda / OpenCL Algorithm Development and Optimization  
- Hardware implementation on CPUs / GPUs / FPGAs  
- Nvidia Jetson family Edge Devices  
- Multimedia flow control with Gstreamer Pipelines  
- Model inference time acceleration with TensorRT, 
- Application pipeline management with Deepstream  
- Synthetic data generation with Nvidia Omniverse, and simulation with Nvidia Isaac Sim  
- Docker, Data Version Control, Minio Storage System, Gitlab   


IOT &amp; AUTOMATION 

- Software Development  
- Hardware Development 
- BLE, LoRa, NFC connectivity 
- RFID, Wireless Sensor Network
          </p>
